<script type="text/javascript">
                    $(document).ready(function() {	
                        function latestWorkHover()
                        {
							var projectDetails = $('#frontpage .front-page-projects-no-description .project-details');
							projectDetails.each(function(){
								$(this).find('.project-content').css('opacity','0');
								$(this).find('.blog-icon').css({'opacity':'0','top':'64','left':'82'});
								$(this).find('.zoom-icon').css({'opacity':'0','top':'64','left':'82'});
								$(this).find('.play-icon').css({'opacity':'0','top':'64','left':'82'});
							});		
							projectDetails.each(function(){
								$(this).hover(function(){
									$(this).find('.project-content').stop().animate({'opacity': 1});	
								}, function(){
									$(this).find('.project-content').stop().animate({'opacity': 0});
								});
							
							});	
							projectDetails.each(function(){
								$(this).hover(function(){
									$(this).find('.blog-icon').stop().animate({'opacity': 1,'top':36,'left':47}, 200, 'swing');
									$(this).find('.zoom-icon').stop().animate({'opacity':1,'top':36,'left':118}, 200, 'swing');
									$(this).find('.play-icon').stop().animate({'opacity':1,'top':36,'left':118}, 200, 'swing');
								}, function(){
									$(this).find('.blog-icon').stop().animate({'opacity': 0,'top':64,'left':82}, 400, 'swing');
									$(this).find('.zoom-icon').stop().animate({'opacity': 0,'top':64,'left':82}, 400, 'swing');
									$(this).find('.play-icon').stop().animate({'opacity': 0,'top':64,'left':82}, 400, 'swing');							
								});	
							});
							if($.browser.msie && $.browser.version.substring(0, 2) === "8.") 
							{
								$('#frontpage .front-page-projects-no-description .project-content').css('background','#333');
							}
                        }
                        $('#frontpage .front-page-projects ul.front-page-projects').bxSlider({displaySlideQty: 4,moveSlideQty: 1,speed:500,onAfterSlide: function(currentSlide, totalSlides){latestWorkHover();} 				});
                    });
                    </script>

	color: #b30404;
	text-decoration: none;

 */

  outline: thin dotted; }

 * Improve readability when focused and also mouse hovered in all browsers.
 */

a:hover {
	color: #ff0000;
	text-decoration: none;
 	outline: 0; 
	transition: all ease-in-out .1s;
	}

                                    <div class="wrapper">
                                        <h2><a href="http://asus.adrenaline.uol.com.br/2017/03/10/48711/asus-anuncia-maximus-ix-extreme-z270-com-monoblock-para-processadores-kaby-lake/">ASUS anuncia Maximus IX Extreme Z270 com monoblock para processadores Kaby Lake</a></h2>
                                        <div class="author">
                                            <p>10/03/2017 16:49                                            <span class="noComm">
                                                <span class="tip tip-down"></span>

                                        </div><!-- .author -->
                                        <p>A ASUS anunciou a placa-m&atilde;e&nbsp;Maximus IX Extreme com chipset Z270 para receber os processadores topo de linha da&nbsp;Intel. A placa vai receber as&nbsp;vers&otilde;es de processadores como o&nbsp;Core i7-7700K de alto desempenho. 			$(window).scroll(function(e){
			
				distancia_menu_template_2 = $('.menu_template_2').offset().top;
				distancia_menu_template_2_hide = parseInt(distancia_menu_template_2) - 10;
				distancia_menu_template_2_show = parseInt(distancia_menu_template_2) + 10;

				/* ================== */
				/* GRUDA MENU NO TOPO */
				/* ================== */
				
				if($(window).scrollTop() >= distancia_menu_template_2_hide && $('.fixed-nav').length <= 0){
					
					newNav = $('.main-nav');
					newNav.addClass('fixed-nav');
					
					newNav.find('.menu').css('margin-top', '5px');
					newNav.find('.menu').css('margin-left', '10px');
					newNav.find('#busca-topo').css('margin-top', '0px');
			
					newNav.find('#logo-topo').css('display', 'none');
			
					newNav.find('.secoes').css('display', 'none');
					newNav.find('.destaque').css('display', 'none');
					newNav.find('.social').css('display', 'none');
					newNav.find('.userLink').css('display', 'none');
					
										newNav.prepend('<div class="adrenaline-small-logo" style="margin-top:7px;margin-left:10px;"><a href="/" class="bigLink"></a></div>');
										newNav.append('<div id="social-roll" class="social" style="margin-top:5px;margin-left:45px;">'+newNav.find('#social_brand').html()+'</div>');
					newNav.append('<div class="back-to-top" style="margin-top:7px;"><span class="icon-adr-trianguloflat-top"></span></div>');
					
					newNav.find('.back-to-top').click(function(e){
						$("html, body").animate({scrollTop:0}, 500, 'easeInOutCirc');
					});
					
					newNav.css({'position': 'fixed', 'top': -50, 'z-index': 50000, 'width': 1020});
					newNav.animate({'top': 0}, 500, 'easeInOutCirc');
					
				} else if($(window).scrollTop() < distancia_menu_template_2_show && $('.fixed-nav').length > 0) {
					
					newNav.removeClass('fixed-nav');
					
					newNav.css({'position': 'relative', 'top': '', 'z-index': '', 'width': ''});
					
										newNav.find('.menu').css('margin-top', '25px');
										newNav.find('#busca-topo').css('margin-top', '18px');
			
					newNav.find('#logo-topo').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.secoes').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.destaque').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.social').css('display', '');
					newNav.find('.userLink').css('display', '');
					
					newNav.find('.adrenaline-small-logo').remove();
					newNav.find('#social-roll').remove();
					newNav.find('.search-button').remove();
					newNav.find('.back-to-top').remove();
					
					if(newNavInterna){
						newNav.find('.secoes-interna').remove();
					}
				}
				
			});

			});
